### systemd/sovereign-alert-relay.service

```ini
# =============================================================
# Sovereign Homelab — Alert Relay Systemd Service
# Repo path: scripts/alerting/systemd/sovereign-alert-relay.service
# Live path: /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-alert-relay.service
#
# Install:
#   cp sovereign-alert-relay.service /etc/systemd/system/
#   systemctl daemon-reload
#   systemctl enable --now sovereign-alert-relay
#
# Check:
#   systemctl status sovereign-alert-relay
#   journalctl -u sovereign-alert-relay -f
# =============================================================

[Unit]
Description=Sovereign Homelab — Alert Relay (Uptime Kuma webhook → HTML email)
Documentation=https://github.com/Mohamed-DN/Sovereign-Homelab
After=network-online.target
Wants=network-online.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
Group=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting
ExecStart=/usr/bin/python3 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/alert_relay.py
Restart=on-failure
RestartSec=10s
StandardOutput=journal
StandardError=journal
SyslogIdentifier=sovereign-alert-relay

# Environment
EnvironmentFile=-/opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env

# Hardening
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true
ProtectSystem=full
ProtectHome=true

# Allow write to state and log directories
ReadWritePaths=/var/lib/sovereign-homelab /var/log/sovereign-homelab /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
```

### Alerting install commands

```bash
# 1. Create directories
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/templates
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/systemd
mkdir -p /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/alerting
mkdir -p /var/log/sovereign-homelab

# 2. Install Python dependencies
pip3 install flask python-dotenv

# 3. Copy scripts (paste content from above into each file)
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/alert_relay.py
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/send_test_alert.py

# 4. Copy templates
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/templates/alert_down.html
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/templates/alert_down.txt
# ... repeat for all 10 templates

# 5. Configure environment
cp /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env.example \
   /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
chmod 600 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
chown root:root /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env

# 6. Test dry-run first
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting
python3 send_test_alert.py --type down --service Immich --dry-run
# Check: ls /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/alerting/dry_run_output/

# 7. Install and start systemd service
cp systemd/sovereign-alert-relay.service /etc/systemd/system/
systemctl daemon-reload
systemctl enable --now sovereign-alert-relay
systemctl status sovereign-alert-relay

# 8. Configure Uptime Kuma webhook
# In Uptime Kuma → Settings → Notifications → Add Notification
# Type: Webhook
# Friendly Name: Alert Relay
# URL: http://127.0.0.1:5001/webhook
# (This assumes Kuma and relay are on the same LXC)

# 9. Send real test
python3 send_test_alert.py --type test
```

---

## 13. Weekly Homelab Report

### Why Python over Bash

| Aspect | Python | Bash |
|---|---|---|
| HTML generation | Native string, template files | Heredoc/echo hell |
| API calls (Proxmox, PBS) | `requests` library, clean JSON | `curl` + `jq` fragile |
| SQLite (Uptime Kuma) | `sqlite3` built-in | External tool needed |
| Error handling | try/except, structured | Set -e, fragile |
| Template rendering | Simple string replace | Complex |
| Email (MIME, HTML+TXT) | `smtplib` + `email` stdlib | External `mutt`/`sendmail` |
| Maintainability | High | Low for complex logic |

**Use Python.**

### Data Sources

| Section | Source | Method |
|---|---|---|
| Downtime/uptime | Uptime Kuma SQLite | Direct SQLite query |
| VM/LXC status | Proxmox API | `requests` + token auth |
| Backup status | PBS API | `requests` + token auth |
| ZFS | zpool/zfs | `subprocess` |
| SMART | smartctl or Scrutiny | `subprocess` or HTTP API |
| Docker containers | docker CLI | `subprocess` |
| System resources | /proc/meminfo, df | `subprocess`/`open()` |
| Errors | journalctl | `subprocess` |
| Failed systemd | systemctl | `subprocess` |
| VPN | headscale CLI | `subprocess` |

### weekly_homelab_report.py

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Homelab Report
Collects data from all local sources and sends a formatted HTML email report.

Repo path: scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py
Live path: /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py

Usage:
    python3 weekly_homelab_report.py              # Send real report
    python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --dry-run    # Generate HTML, save to disk
    python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --send-test  # Send single test email

Environment file:
    /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env

Output (dry-run):
    /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output/

Logs:
    /var/log/sovereign-homelab/weekly_report.log

Dependencies:
    pip3 install requests python-dotenv
"""

import os
import sys
import re
import json
import time
import logging
import sqlite3
import smtplib
import argparse
import subprocess
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

# ── Optional requests ──────────────────────────────────────────
try:
    import requests
    requests.packages.urllib3.disable_warnings()
    HAS_REQUESTS = True
except ImportError:
    HAS_REQUESTS = False

try:
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
except ImportError:
    print("ERROR: pip3 install python-dotenv requests")
    sys.exit(1)

# ── Environment ────────────────────────────────────────────────
_env_path = Path(__file__).parent / ".env"
load_dotenv(_env_path)

SMTP_HOST       = os.getenv("SMTP_HOST", "smtp.gmail.com")
SMTP_PORT       = int(os.getenv("SMTP_PORT", "587"))
SMTP_USERNAME   = os.getenv("SMTP_USERNAME", "")
SMTP_PASSWORD   = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD", "")
EMAIL_FROM      = os.getenv("EMAIL_FROM", SMTP_USERNAME)
EMAIL_TO        = os.getenv("EMAIL_TO", "")
HOMELAB_NAME    = os.getenv("HOMELAB_NAME", "Sovereign Homelab")

PROXMOX_HOST    = os.getenv("PROXMOX_HOST", "proxmox.internal")
PROXMOX_TOKEN_ID     = os.getenv("PROXMOX_TOKEN_ID", "")
PROXMOX_TOKEN_SECRET = os.getenv("PROXMOX_TOKEN_SECRET", "")

PBS_HOST        = os.getenv("PBS_HOST", "pbs.internal")
PBS_TOKEN_ID    = os.getenv("PBS_TOKEN_ID", "")
PBS_TOKEN_SECRET = os.getenv("PBS_TOKEN_SECRET", "")

KUMA_DB_PATH    = os.getenv("KUMA_DB_PATH", "/opt/uptime-kuma/data/kuma.db")

# ── Paths ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
BASE_DIR     = Path(__file__).parent
TEMPLATE_DIR = BASE_DIR / "templates"
STATE_DIR    = Path("/var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting")
LOG_DIR      = Path("/var/log/sovereign-homelab")
LOG_PATH     = LOG_DIR / "weekly_report.log"
DRYRUN_DIR   = STATE_DIR / "dry_run_output"

for d in [STATE_DIR, LOG_DIR, DRYRUN_DIR]:
    d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# ── Logging ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S",
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler(LOG_PATH, encoding="utf-8"),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
    ],
)
logger = logging.getLogger("weekly_report")

# ── Time range: last 7 days ────────────────────────────────────
NOW        = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc)
WEEK_START = NOW - timedelta(days=7)
WEEK_START_TS = WEEK_START.timestamp()

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# DATA COLLECTION FUNCTIONS
# Each function returns a dict with collected data.
# On failure, returns dict with "error" key.
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

def collect_uptime_kuma() -> dict:
    """Query Uptime Kuma SQLite for monitor statuses and incidents."""
    result = {
        "monitors": [],
        "incidents": [],
        "total_down_events": 0,
        "error": None,
    }
    db_path = Path(KUMA_DB_PATH)
    if not db_path.exists():
        # Try docker volume path
        alt_path = Path("/var/lib/docker/volumes/uptime-kuma_data/_data/kuma.db")
        if alt_path.exists():
            db_path = alt_path
        else:
            result["error"] = f"Uptime Kuma DB not found at {KUMA_DB_PATH}"
            logger.warning(result["error"])
            return result
    try:
        with sqlite3.connect(str(db_path), timeout=10) as conn:
            conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row

            # Current monitor statuses
            monitors = conn.execute("""
                SELECT m.id, m.name, m.type, m.url, m.active,
                       h.status, h.time as last_check, h.msg
                FROM monitor m
                LEFT JOIN heartbeat h ON h.monitor_id = m.id
                    AND h.time = (SELECT MAX(time) FROM heartbeat WHERE monitor_id = m.id)
                WHERE m.active = 1
                ORDER BY m.name
            """).fetchall()
            result["monitors"] = [dict(r) for r in monitors]

            # Downtime events in last 7 days
            incidents = conn.execute("""
                SELECT m.name as service,
                       COUNT(*) as down_events,
                       SUM(CASE WHEN h2.status = 0
                               THEN COALESCE(
                                   (SELECT MIN(h3.time) FROM heartbeat h3
                                    WHERE h3.monitor_id = h2.monitor_id
                                    AND h3.time > h2.time AND h3.status = 1),
                                   strftime('%s','now')
                               ) - h2.time
                               ELSE 0 END) as total_down_seconds
                FROM heartbeat h2
                JOIN monitor m ON m.id = h2.monitor_id
                WHERE h2.status = 0
                  AND h2.time >= ?
                GROUP BY m.id, m.name
                ORDER BY down_events DESC
            """, (int(WEEK_START_TS),)).fetchall()
            result["incidents"] = [dict(r) for r in incidents]
            result["total_down_events"] = sum(r["down_events"] for r in result["incidents"])

    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
        logger.warning(f"Uptime Kuma collection failed: {exc}")

    return result

def collect_proxmox() -> dict:
    """Query Proxmox API for node and VM/LXC status."""
    result = {
        "node_status": {},
        "guests": [],
        "error": None,
    }
    if not HAS_REQUESTS:
        result["error"] = "requests library not installed"
        return result
    if not PROXMOX_TOKEN_ID or not PROXMOX_TOKEN_SECRET:
        result["error"] = "Proxmox API token not configured"
        logger.info("Proxmox API token not configured — skipping")
        return result

    base = f"https://{PROXMOX_HOST}:8006/api2/json"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"PVEAPIToken={PROXMOX_TOKEN_ID}={PROXMOX_TOKEN_SECRET}"}

    try:
        # Node status
        node_resp = requests.get(
            f"{base}/nodes", headers=headers, verify=False, timeout=10
        )
        if node_resp.ok:
            nodes = node_resp.json().get("data", [])
            if nodes:
                node_name = nodes[0].get("node", "pve")
                stat_resp = requests.get(
                    f"{base}/nodes/{node_name}/status",
                    headers=headers, verify=False, timeout=10
                )
                if stat_resp.ok:
                    result["node_status"] = stat_resp.json().get("data", {})

        # VM list
        for vtype in ["qemu", "lxc"]:
            for node in nodes:
                nname = node.get("node", "pve")
                resp = requests.get(
                    f"{base}/nodes/{nname}/{vtype}",
                    headers=headers, verify=False, timeout=10
                )
                if resp.ok:
                    for g in resp.json().get("data", []):
                        g["node"]   = nname
                        g["type"]   = vtype
                        result["guests"].append(g)

    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
        logger.warning(f"Proxmox collection failed: {exc}")

    return result

def collect_pbs() -> dict:
    """Query PBS API for backup job status."""
    result = {
        "datastores": [],
        "tasks": [],
        "failed_backups": [],
        "error": None,
    }
    if not HAS_REQUESTS:
        result["error"] = "requests library not installed"
        return result
    if not PBS_TOKEN_ID or not PBS_TOKEN_SECRET:
        result["error"] = "PBS API token not configured"
        logger.info("PBS API token not configured — skipping")
        return result

    base    = f"https://{PBS_HOST}:8007/api2/json"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"PBSAPIToken={PBS_TOKEN_ID}:{PBS_TOKEN_SECRET}"}

    try:
        # Datastores
        ds_resp = requests.get(f"{base}/admin/datastore",
                               headers=headers, verify=False, timeout=10)
        if ds_resp.ok:
            result["datastores"] = ds_resp.json().get("data", [])

        # Recent tasks (last 7 days)
        tasks_resp = requests.get(
            f"{base}/nodes/localhost/tasks?limit=200",
            headers=headers, verify=False, timeout=10
        )
        if tasks_resp.ok:
            tasks = tasks_resp.json().get("data", [])
            recent = [t for t in tasks if t.get("starttime", 0) >= WEEK_START_TS]
            result["tasks"] = recent
            result["failed_backups"] = [
                t for t in recent
                if t.get("status") and "error" in str(t.get("status", "")).lower()
            ]

    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
        logger.warning(f"PBS collection failed: {exc}")

    return result

def collect_zfs() -> dict:
    """Run zpool status and zfs list."""
    result = {"pools": [], "datasets": [], "raw_status": "", "error": None}
    try:
        zpool = subprocess.run(
            ["zpool", "status", "-v"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=15
        )
        result["raw_status"] = zpool.stdout
        # Parse pool health
        for line in zpool.stdout.splitlines():
            m = re.match(r"\s*pool:\s+(\S+)", line)
            if m:
                pool_name = m.group(1)
            m2 = re.match(r"\s*state:\s+(\S+)", line)
            if m2:
                result["pools"].append({
                    "name":   pool_name if "pool_name" in dir() else "unknown",
                    "state":  m2.group(1),
                    "healthy": m2.group(1) == "ONLINE",
                })
    except FileNotFoundError:
        result["error"] = "zpool not found — not a ZFS host"
    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
    return result

def collect_smart() -> dict:
    """Try to query Scrutiny API for SMART data."""
    result = {"devices": [], "failing": [], "error": None}
    if not HAS_REQUESTS:
        result["error"] = "requests not installed"
        return result
    try:
        resp = requests.get(
            "http://disks.internal/api/summary",
            timeout=10
        )
        if resp.ok:
            data = resp.json()
            devices = data.get("data", {}).get("summary", {})
            for dev_id, dev_data in devices.items():
                smart = dev_data.get("smart", {})
                status = dev_data.get("device", {})
                entry = {
                    "name":   status.get("device_name", dev_id),
                    "model":  status.get("model_name", ""),
                    "status": smart.get("Status", "unknown"),
                    "failing": smart.get("Status", "") in ["failed", "warn"],
                }
                result["devices"].append(entry)
                if entry["failing"]:
                    result["failing"].append(entry)
    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
        logger.info(f"Scrutiny collection failed (non-critical): {exc}")
    return result

def collect_docker() -> dict:
    """Get Docker container status from host."""
    result = {"containers": [], "unhealthy": [], "error": None}
    try:
        proc = subprocess.run(
            ["docker", "ps", "-a",
             "--format", "{{.Names}}|{{.Status}}|{{.Image}}|{{.RunningFor}}"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=15
        )
        for line in proc.stdout.splitlines():
            parts = line.split("|")
            if len(parts) < 4:
                continue
            name, status, image, running_for = parts[:4]
            entry = {
                "name":        name.strip(),
                "status":      status.strip(),
                "image":       image.strip(),
                "running_for": running_for.strip(),
                "healthy":     status.strip().lower().startswith("up"),
                "restarting":  "restarting" in status.lower(),
                "exited":      "exited" in status.lower(),
            }
            result["containers"].append(entry)
            if not entry["healthy"]:
                result["unhealthy"].append(entry)
    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
    return result

def collect_system() -> dict:
    """Collect system-level metrics (disk, memory, load)."""
    result = {
        "disk_usage":  [],
        "mem_total_gb": 0,
        "mem_used_gb":  0,
        "mem_pct":      0,
        "load_avg":    "",
        "failed_units": [],
        "error": None,
    }
    try:
        # Disk
        df = subprocess.run(
            ["df", "-h", "--output=source,size,used,avail,pcent,target"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10
        )
        for line in df.stdout.splitlines()[1:]:
            parts = line.split()
            if len(parts) >= 6 and parts[0].startswith("/dev"):
                pct_str = parts[4].replace("%","")
                try:
                    pct = int(pct_str)
                except ValueError:
                    pct = 0
                result["disk_usage"].append({
                    "device": parts[0],
                    "size":   parts[1],
                    "used":   parts[2],
                    "avail":  parts[3],
                    "pct":    pct,
                    "mount":  parts[5],
                    "warning": pct >= 70,
                    "critical": pct >= 85,
                })

        # Memory
        with open("/proc/meminfo") as f:
            meminfo = {
                line.split(":")[0]: int(line.split(":")[1].strip().split()[0])
                for line in f if ":" in line
            }
        total_kb    = meminfo.get("MemTotal", 1)
        avail_kb    = meminfo.get("MemAvailable", total_kb)
        used_kb     = total_kb - avail_kb
        result["mem_total_gb"] = round(total_kb / 1024 / 1024, 1)
        result["mem_used_gb"]  = round(used_kb  / 1024 / 1024, 1)
        result["mem_pct"]      = round(used_kb  / total_kb * 100, 1)

        # Load average
        with open("/proc/loadavg") as f:
            result["load_avg"] = f.read().split()[:3]
            result["load_avg"] = " / ".join(result["load_avg"])

        # Failed systemd units
        sctl = subprocess.run(
            ["systemctl", "--failed", "--no-legend", "--plain"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10
        )
        for line in sctl.stdout.splitlines():
            parts = line.split()
            if parts:
                result["failed_units"].append(parts[0])

    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
        logger.warning(f"System collection failed: {exc}")
    return result

def collect_journal_errors() -> dict:
    """Get recent critical errors from journalctl."""
    result = {"errors": [], "error": None}
    try:
        proc = subprocess.run(
            ["journalctl",
             "-p", "err",
             "--since", WEEK_START.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
             "--no-pager",
             "-n", "50",
             "-o", "short-iso"],
            capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=20
        )
        lines = [l for l in proc.stdout.splitlines() if l.strip()]
        result["errors"] = lines[:30]
    except Exception as exc:
        result["error"] = str(exc)
    return result

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# HTML GENERATION
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

def fmt_bytes(n: float) -> str:
    for unit in ["B", "KB", "MB", "GB", "TB"]:
        if n < 1024:
            return f"{n:.1f} {unit}"
        n /= 1024
    return f"{n:.1f} PB"

def status_dot(healthy: bool) -> str:
    return "🟢" if healthy else "🔴"

def status_badge_html(label: str, color: str, bg: str) -> str:
    return (
        f'<span style="display:inline-block;background-color:{bg};'
        f'color:{color};font-size:10px;font-weight:700;padding:3px 10px;'
        f'border-radius:12px;letter-spacing:0.08em;text-transform:uppercase;">'
        f'{label}</span>'
    )

def build_report(data: dict, test_mode: bool = False) -> tuple[str, str]:
    """Build HTML and TXT report from collected data."""
    kuma  = data.get("uptime_kuma", {})
    prox  = data.get("proxmox", {})
    pbs   = data.get("pbs", {})
    zfs   = data.get("zfs", {})
    smart = data.get("smart", {})
    dock  = data.get("docker", {})
    sys_  = data.get("system", {})
    jrnl  = data.get("journal", {})

    period_str = (
        f"{WEEK_START.strftime('%a %d %b')} – {NOW.strftime('%a %d %b %Y')}"
    )
    generated = NOW.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M UTC")

    # ── Determine overall status ──────────────────────────────
    critical_count = 0
    warning_count  = 0
    actions        = []  # list of (priority, action_html, action_txt)

    # Check ZFS
    for pool in zfs.get("pools", []):
        if not pool["healthy"]:
            critical_count += 1
            act_txt = f"ZFS pool '{pool['name']}' state: {pool['state']} — run: zpool status -v"
            actions.append(("P0", f"<strong>ZFS pool <code>{pool['name']}</code></strong> is in state <code>{pool['state']}</code> — run: <code>zpool status -v</code>", act_txt))

    # Check SMART
    for dev in smart.get("failing", []):
        critical_count += 1
        act_txt = f"SMART failure: {dev['name']} ({dev['model']}) — check Scrutiny: http://disks.internal"
        actions.append(("P0", f"SMART failure: <strong>{dev['name']}</strong> ({dev['model']}) — <a href='http://disks.internal' style='color:#93c5fd;'>check Scrutiny</a>", act_txt))

    # Check PBS failed backups
    for task in pbs.get("failed_backups", []):
        critical_count += 1
        guest = task.get("id", "unknown")
        act_txt = f"PBS backup failed for {guest} — check PBS: https://pbs.internal:8007"
        actions.append(("P0", f"PBS backup failed for <strong>{guest}</strong> — <a href='https://pbs.internal:8007' style='color:#93c5fd;'>check PBS</a>", act_txt))

    # Check Uptime Kuma incidents
    for inc in kuma.get("incidents", []):
        if inc.get("down_events", 0) > 3:
            critical_count += 1
            svc = inc.get("service", "?")
            act_txt = f"{svc} had {inc['down_events']} down events this week — investigate"
            actions.append(("P1", f"<strong>{svc}</strong> had {inc['down_events']} down events this week — <a href='http://status.internal' style='color:#93c5fd;'>check Kuma</a>", act_txt))
        elif inc.get("down_events", 0) > 0:
            warning_count += 1

    # Check disk usage
    for disk in sys_.get("disk_usage", []):
        if disk.get("critical"):
            critical_count += 1
            act_txt = f"Disk {disk['mount']} at {disk['pct']}% — free up space ASAP"
            actions.append(("P0", f"Disk <strong>{disk['mount']}</strong> at <strong>{disk['pct']}%</strong> — free up space immediately", act_txt))
        elif disk.get("warning"):
            warning_count += 1
            act_txt = f"Disk {disk['mount']} at {disk['pct']}% — monitor and plan cleanup"
            actions.append(("P1", f"Disk <strong>{disk['mount']}</strong> at <strong>{disk['pct']}%</strong> — plan cleanup this week", act_txt))

    # Check failed systemd units
    for unit in sys_.get("failed_units", []):
        warning_count += 1
        act_txt = f"Systemd unit failed: {unit} — run: systemctl status {unit}"
        actions.append(("P1", f"Systemd unit failed: <code>{unit}</code> — <code>systemctl status {unit}</code>", act_txt))

    # Check PBS errors
    if pbs.get("error") is None and not pbs.get("datastores"):
        warning_count += 1
        actions.append(("P1", "PBS API returned no datastores — verify PBS is running and token is valid", "PBS API returned no datastores"))

    # Overall status
    if critical_count > 0:
        overall_label = "🔴 CRITICAL"
        overall_color = "#dc2626"
        overall_bg    = "#450a0a"
    elif warning_count > 0:
        overall_label = "🟡 WARNING"
        overall_color = "#d97706"
        overall_bg    = "#451a03"
    else:
        overall_label = "🟢 HEALTHY"
        overall_color = "#16a34a"
        overall_bg    = "#052e16"

    # Sort actions by priority
    priority_order = {"P0": 0, "P1": 1, "P2": 2}
    actions.sort(key=lambda x: priority_order.get(x[0], 9))

    # ── Load template ──────────────────────────────────────────
    html_tpl = (TEMPLATE_DIR / "weekly_report.html").read_text("utf-8") \
               if (TEMPLATE_DIR / "weekly_report.html").exists() \
               else _default_html_template()
    txt_tpl  = (TEMPLATE_DIR / "weekly_report.txt").read_text("utf-8") \
               if (TEMPLATE_DIR / "weekly_report.txt").exists() \
               else _default_txt_template()

    # ── Build downtime table ───────────────────────────────────
    downtime_rows_html = ""
    downtime_rows_txt  = ""
    for inc in kuma.get("incidents", []):
        svc   = inc.get("service", "?")
        evts  = inc.get("down_events", 0)
        secs  = int(inc.get("total_down_seconds", 0))
        dur   = f"{secs//60}m" if secs < 3600 else f"{secs//3600}h {(secs%3600)//60}m"
        color = "#ef4444" if evts > 3 else "#fbbf24"
        downtime_rows_html += (
            f'<tr><td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#e2e8f0;">{svc}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:{color};font-weight:600;text-align:center;">{evts}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#94a3b8;text-align:center;">{dur}</td>'
            f'</tr>\n'
        )
        downtime_rows_txt += f"  {svc:<30} {evts:>3} events   {dur}\n"

    if not downtime_rows_html:
        downtime_rows_html = '<tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:12px;text-align:center;color:#22c55e;">✅ No downtime this week</td></tr>'
        downtime_rows_txt  = "  No downtime this week.\n"

    # ── Build backup table ─────────────────────────────────────
    backup_rows_html = ""
    backup_rows_txt  = ""
    for task in pbs.get("tasks", [])[:10]:
        guest  = task.get("id", "?")
        ts     = task.get("starttime", 0)
        dt_str = datetime.fromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%m/%d %H:%M") if ts else "?"
        status = task.get("status", "unknown")
        ok     = "error" not in str(status).lower()
        dot    = "🟢" if ok else "🔴"
        s_col  = "#22c55e" if ok else "#ef4444"
        backup_rows_html += (
            f'<tr><td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#e2e8f0;">{dot} {guest}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#94a3b8;">{dt_str}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:{s_col};">{status[:30]}</td>'
            f'</tr>\n'
        )
        backup_rows_txt += f"  {dot} {guest:<25} {dt_str}  {status[:30]}\n"

    if not backup_rows_html:
        backup_rows_html = '<tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:12px;text-align:center;color:#64748b;">PBS API not configured or no tasks found</td></tr>'
        backup_rows_txt  = "  PBS data not available.\n"

    # ── Build disk table ───────────────────────────────────────
    disk_rows_html = ""
    disk_rows_txt  = ""
    for disk in sys_.get("disk_usage", []):
        pct   = disk.get("pct", 0)
        color = "#ef4444" if pct >= 85 else ("#fbbf24" if pct >= 70 else "#22c55e")
        bar_w = min(pct, 100)
        disk_rows_html += (
            f'<tr><td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#e2e8f0;">{disk["mount"]}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;color:#94a3b8;">{disk["used"]} / {disk["size"]}</td>'
            f'<td style="padding:8px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;">'
            f'<div style="background:#334155;border-radius:4px;height:8px;width:120px;display:inline-block;">'
            f'<div style="background:{color};height:8px;border-radius:4px;width:{bar_w}%;"></div></div>'
            f'&nbsp;<span style="color:{color};font-size:12px;font-weight:600;">{pct}%</span></td>'
            f'</tr>\n'
        )
        indicator = "🔴" if pct >= 85 else ("🟡" if pct >= 70 else "🟢")
        disk_rows_txt += f"  {indicator} {disk['mount']:<20} {disk['used']:>6} / {disk['size']:>6}  ({pct}%)\n"

    # ── Build actions list ─────────────────────────────────────
    actions_html = ""
    actions_txt  = ""
    for i, (prio, html_act, txt_act) in enumerate(actions, 1):
        p_color = {"P0":"#dc2626","P1":"#d97706","P2":"#2563eb"}.get(prio,"#64748b")
        p_bg    = {"P0":"#450a0a","P1":"#451a03","P2":"#172554"}.get(prio,"#1e293b")
        actions_html += (
            f'<tr><td style="padding:10px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;vertical-align:top;">'
            f'<span style="background:{p_color};color:#fff;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;'
            f'padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;">{prio}</span></td>'
            f'<td style="padding:10px 12px;border-bottom:1px solid #1e293b;font-size:13px;color:#e2e8f0;">'
            f'{i}. {html_act}</td></tr>\n'
        )
        actions_txt += f"  [{prio}] {i}. {txt_act}\n"

    if not actions_html:
        actions_html = '<tr><td colspan="2" style="padding:16px;text-align:center;color:#22c55e;font-size:14px;">✅ No actions required — everything looks healthy!</td></tr>'
        actions_txt  = "  No actions required — everything looks healthy!\n"

    # ── Summary stats ──────────────────────────────────────────
    total_monitors = len(kuma.get("monitors", []))
    monitors_down  = sum(1 for m in kuma.get("monitors", []) if m.get("status") == 0)
    monitors_up    = total_monitors - monitors_down
    uptime_pct     = round(monitors_up / total_monitors * 100, 1) if total_monitors else 100

    failed_backups_count = len(pbs.get("failed_backups", []))
    zfs_pools      = zfs.get("pools", [])
    zfs_healthy    = all(p["healthy"] for p in zfs_pools) if zfs_pools else None
    zfs_status     = ("🟢 ONLINE" if zfs_healthy else "🔴 DEGRADED") if zfs_pools else "⚪ N/A"

    mem_pct        = sys_.get("mem_pct", 0)
    load_avg       = sys_.get("load_avg", "N/A")
    failed_units   = sys_.get("failed_units", [])

    test_banner = ""
    if test_mode:
        test_banner = (
            '<tr><td colspan="1" bgcolor="#172554" style="background:#172554;'
            'padding:12px 32px;text-align:center;border-bottom:1px solid #1d4ed8;">'
            '<p style="margin:0;font-size:12px;color:#93c5fd;font-weight:700;">'
            '🔵 TEST MODE — This is a test report. Data may be incomplete.</p></td></tr>'
        )

    # ── Substitute template ────────────────────────────────────
    ctx = {
        "HOMELAB_NAME":          HOMELAB_NAME,
        "PERIOD":                period_str,
        "GENERATED":             generated,
        "OVERALL_LABEL":         overall_label,
        "OVERALL_COLOR":         overall_color,
        "OVERALL_BG":            overall_bg,
        "TOTAL_MONITORS":        str(total_monitors),
        "MONITORS_UP":           str(monitors_up),
        "MONITORS_DOWN":         str(monitors_down),
        "UPTIME_PCT":            str(uptime_pct),
        "TOTAL_DOWN_EVENTS":     str(kuma.get("total_down_events", 0)),
        "FAILED_BACKUPS":        str(failed_backups_count),
        "ZFS_STATUS":            zfs_status,
        "MEM_PCT":               str(mem_pct),
        "LOAD_AVG":              load_avg,
        "FAILED_UNITS":          str(len(failed_units)),
        "CRITICAL_COUNT":        str(critical_count),
        "WARNING_COUNT":         str(warning_count),
        "DOWNTIME_ROWS":         downtime_rows_html,
        "BACKUP_ROWS":           backup_rows_html,
        "DISK_ROWS":             disk_rows_html,
        "ACTIONS_ROWS":          actions_html,
        "DOWNTIME_ROWS_TXT":     downtime_rows_txt,
        "BACKUP_ROWS_TXT":       backup_rows_txt,
        "DISK_ROWS_TXT":         disk_rows_txt,
        "ACTIONS_TXT":           actions_txt,
        "TEST_BANNER":           test_banner,
        "YEAR":                  str(NOW.year),
        "KUMA_URL":              "http://status.internal",
        "PROXMOX_URL":           f"https://{PROXMOX_HOST}:8006",
        "PBS_URL":               f"https://{PBS_HOST}:8007",
        "DASHBOARD_URL":         "http://dash.internal",
    }

    html = html_tpl
    txt  = txt_tpl
    for k, v in ctx.items():
        html = html.replace(f"{{{{{k}}}}}", v)
        txt  = txt.replace(f"{{{{{k}}}}}", v)

    return html, txt

def _default_html_template() -> str:
    """Minimal fallback HTML template if file not found."""
    return """<!DOCTYPE html>
<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0">
<title>{{HOMELAB_NAME}} Weekly Report</title></head>
<body style="margin:0;padding:0;background:#0f172a;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">
<table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" bgcolor="#0f172a">
<tr><td align="center" style="padding:20px 12px;">
<table width="640" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="max-width:640px;width:100%;border-radius:16px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid #334155;">
{{TEST_BANNER}}
<tr><td bgcolor="#0ea5e9" style="background:#0ea5e9;padding:32px 40px;text-align:center;">
  <p style="margin:0 0 6px;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.75);letter-spacing:.12em;text-transform:uppercase;">{{HOMELAB_NAME}}</p>
  <h1 style="margin:0;font-size:26px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;">Weekly Status Report</h1>
  <p style="margin:8px 0 0;font-size:13px;color:#bae6fd;">{{PERIOD}}</p>
  <p style="margin:4px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.5);">Generated: {{GENERATED}}</p>
</td></tr>
<!-- Overall Status -->
<tr><td bgcolor="{{OVERALL_BG}}" style="background:{{OVERALL_BG}};padding:16px 40px;text-align:center;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <span style="font-size:20px;color:{{OVERALL_COLOR}};font-weight:700;">{{OVERALL_LABEL}}</span>
  &nbsp;&nbsp;
  <span style="font-size:13px;color:#64748b;">{{CRITICAL_COUNT}} critical · {{WARNING_COUNT}} warnings</span>
</td></tr>
<!-- Stats Cards -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#1e293b" style="background:#1e293b;padding:20px 32px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
  <tr>
    <td style="text-align:center;padding:8px;">
      <p style="margin:0;font-size:24px;font-weight:700;color:#22c55e;">{{UPTIME_PCT}}%</p>
      <p style="margin:2px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;">Uptime</p>
    </td>
    <td style="text-align:center;padding:8px;border-left:1px solid #334155;">
      <p style="margin:0;font-size:24px;font-weight:700;color:#ef4444;">{{TOTAL_DOWN_EVENTS}}</p>
      <p style="margin:2px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;">Down Events</p>
    </td>
    <td style="text-align:center;padding:8px;border-left:1px solid #334155;">
      <p style="margin:0;font-size:24px;font-weight:700;color:{{OVERALL_COLOR}};">{{FAILED_BACKUPS}}</p>
      <p style="margin:2px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;">Failed Backups</p>
    </td>
    <td style="text-align:center;padding:8px;border-left:1px solid #334155;">
      <p style="margin:0;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:#e2e8f0;">{{ZFS_STATUS}}</p>
      <p style="margin:2px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;">ZFS</p>
    </td>
  </tr>
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- What You Need To Do -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#0f172a" style="background:#0f172a;padding:20px 32px 8px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <p style="margin:0 0 12px;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9;letter-spacing:.04em;">⚡ WHAT YOU NEED TO DO</p>
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="background:#1e293b;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">
  {{ACTIONS_ROWS}}
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- Downtime Table -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#0f172a" style="background:#0f172a;padding:20px 32px 8px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <p style="margin:0 0 12px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9;">📊 DOWNTIME THIS WEEK</p>
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="background:#1e293b;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">
  <tr><th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Service</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Events</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Total Down</th></tr>
  {{DOWNTIME_ROWS}}
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- Backup Table -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#0f172a" style="background:#0f172a;padding:20px 32px 8px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <p style="margin:0 0 12px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9;">💾 BACKUP STATUS</p>
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="background:#1e293b;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">
  <tr><th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Guest</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Last Run</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Status</th></tr>
  {{BACKUP_ROWS}}
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- Disk Table -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#0f172a" style="background:#0f172a;padding:20px 32px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <p style="margin:0 0 12px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9;">🖴 STORAGE USAGE</p>
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="background:#1e293b;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">
  <tr><th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Mount</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Used / Size</th>
      <th style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;">Usage</th></tr>
  {{DISK_ROWS}}
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- System Info -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#1e293b" style="background:#1e293b;padding:16px 32px;border-bottom:1px solid #334155;">
  <table width="100%" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
  <tr>
    <td style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:12px;color:#64748b;">Memory:</td>
    <td style="padding:4px;font-size:12px;color:#e2e8f0;font-weight:600;">{{MEM_PCT}}% used</td>
    <td style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:12px;color:#64748b;">Load avg:</td>
    <td style="padding:4px;font-size:12px;color:#e2e8f0;">{{LOAD_AVG}}</td>
    <td style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:12px;color:#64748b;">Failed units:</td>
    <td style="padding:4px;font-size:12px;color:#ef4444;font-weight:600;">{{FAILED_UNITS}}</td>
  </tr>
  </table>
</td></tr>
<!-- Footer -->
<tr><td bgcolor="#0f172a" style="background:#0f172a;padding:16px 40px;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #1e293b;">
  <p style="margin:0;font-size:11px;color:#334155;">{{HOMELAB_NAME}} · Weekly Report · {{PERIOD}} · Generated {{GENERATED}}</p>
  <p style="margin:4px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#1e293b;">
    <a href="{{DASHBOARD_URL}}" style="color:#334155;text-decoration:none;">Dashboard</a> ·
    <a href="{{KUMA_URL}}" style="color:#334155;text-decoration:none;">Uptime Kuma</a> ·
    <a href="{{PBS_URL}}" style="color:#334155;text-decoration:none;">PBS</a>
  </p>
</td></tr>
</table>
</td></tr>
</table>
</body></html>"""

def _default_txt_template() -> str:
    return """
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  {{HOMELAB_NAME}} — Weekly Status Report
  {{PERIOD}}
  Generated: {{GENERATED}}
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Overall Status: {{OVERALL_LABEL}}
  Critical issues: {{CRITICAL_COUNT}}
  Warnings:        {{WARNING_COUNT}}

Summary:
  Uptime:          {{UPTIME_PCT}}%  ({{MONITORS_UP}}/{{TOTAL_MONITORS}} monitors up)
  Down events:     {{TOTAL_DOWN_EVENTS}}
  Failed backups:  {{FAILED_BACKUPS}}
  ZFS:             {{ZFS_STATUS}}
  Memory:          {{MEM_PCT}}% used
  Load avg:        {{LOAD_AVG}}
  Failed units:    {{FAILED_UNITS}}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
⚡ WHAT YOU NEED TO DO
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

{{ACTIONS_TXT}}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
📊 DOWNTIME THIS WEEK
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  Service                        Events   Total Down
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
{{DOWNTIME_ROWS_TXT}}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
💾 BACKUP STATUS (last 10 tasks)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

{{BACKUP_ROWS_TXT}}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
🖴 STORAGE USAGE
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

{{DISK_ROWS_TXT}}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Dashboard:   {{DASHBOARD_URL}}
Uptime Kuma: {{KUMA_URL}}
Proxmox:     {{PROXMOX_URL}}
PBS:         {{PBS_URL}}

{{HOMELAB_NAME}} · Weekly Report · {{YEAR}}
"""

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# EMAIL SENDING
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

def send_report_email(subject: str, html: str, txt: str) -> bool:
    if not all([SMTP_HOST, SMTP_USERNAME, SMTP_PASSWORD, EMAIL_TO]):
        logger.error("SMTP not configured — check .env")
        return False
    try:
        msg = MIMEMultipart("alternative")
        msg["Subject"]          = subject
        msg["From"]             = f"{HOMELAB_NAME} <{EMAIL_FROM}>"
        msg["To"]               = EMAIL_TO
        msg["X-Homelab-Source"] = "sovereign-homelab-weekly-report"
        msg.attach(MIMEText(txt,  "plain", "utf-8"))
        msg.attach(MIMEText(html, "html",  "utf-8"))
        with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_HOST, SMTP_PORT) as smtp:
            smtp.ehlo()
            smtp.starttls()
            smtp.login(SMTP_USERNAME, SMTP_PASSWORD)
            smtp.sendmail(EMAIL_FROM, [EMAIL_TO], msg.as_string())
        logger.info(f"Weekly report sent to {EMAIL_TO}")
        return True
    except Exception as exc:
        logger.error(f"Weekly report email failed: {exc}")
        return False

def save_dry_run_output(subject: str, html: str, txt: str) -> None:
    DRYRUN_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    ts = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    (DRYRUN_DIR / f"{ts}_subject.txt").write_text(subject, "utf-8")
    (DRYRUN_DIR / f"{ts}_report.html").write_text(html, "utf-8")
    (DRYRUN_DIR / f"{ts}_report.txt").write_text(txt, "utf-8")
    logger.info(f"Dry-run output saved to: {DRYRUN_DIR}")
    print(f"\nDry-run mode — output saved to: {DRYRUN_DIR}/")
    print(f"  HTML: {ts}_report.html")
    print(f"  TXT:  {ts}_report.txt")
    print(f"  Open: xdg-open {DRYRUN_DIR}/{ts}_report.html")

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# MAIN
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Sovereign Homelab Weekly Report")
    parser.add_argument("--dry-run",   action="store_true", help="Generate HTML, save to disk, no email")
    parser.add_argument("--send-test", action="store_true", help="Send test email with [TEST] prefix")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    test_mode = args.send_test

    logger.info("═" * 60)
    logger.info(f"Weekly report started — dry_run={args.dry_run} send_test={args.send_test}")
    logger.info(f"Period: {WEEK_START.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} → {NOW.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")

    # ── Collect data ───────────────────────────────────────────
    logger.info("Collecting Uptime Kuma data...")
    kuma_data = collect_uptime_kuma()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(kuma_data.get('monitors', []))} monitors, "
                f"{len(kuma_data.get('incidents', []))} with downtime")

    logger.info("Collecting Proxmox data...")
    prox_data = collect_proxmox()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(prox_data.get('guests', []))} guests, error={prox_data.get('error')}")

    logger.info("Collecting PBS data...")
    pbs_data = collect_pbs()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(pbs_data.get('tasks', []))}
User: e il resto ? ce altro ?
Model: # Sovereign Homelab Repository Audit — PARTE 2 (continuazione)

> Continuo esattamente da dove si è interrotto il main() di weekly_homelab_report.py

---

### weekly_homelab_report.py — CONTINUAZIONE main()

```python
    logger.info("Collecting PBS data...")
    pbs_data = collect_pbs()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(pbs_data.get('tasks', []))} tasks, "
                f"{len(pbs_data.get('failed_backups', []))} failed, error={pbs_data.get('error')}")

    logger.info("Collecting ZFS data...")
    zfs_data = collect_zfs()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(zfs_data.get('pools', []))} pools, error={zfs_data.get('error')}")

    logger.info("Collecting SMART/Scrutiny data...")
    smart_data = collect_smart()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(smart_data.get('devices', []))} devices, "
                f"{len(smart_data.get('failing', []))} failing")

    logger.info("Collecting Docker data...")
    dock_data = collect_docker()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(dock_data.get('containers', []))} containers, "
                f"{len(dock_data.get('unhealthy', []))} unhealthy")

    logger.info("Collecting system metrics...")
    sys_data = collect_system()
    logger.info(f"  → mem={sys_data.get('mem_pct')}%, "
                f"failed_units={len(sys_data.get('failed_units', []))}")

    logger.info("Collecting journal errors...")
    jrnl_data = collect_journal_errors()
    logger.info(f"  → {len(jrnl_data.get('errors', []))} error lines")

    # ── Bundle all data ────────────────────────────────────────
    all_data = {
        "uptime_kuma": kuma_data,
        "proxmox":     prox_data,
        "pbs":         pbs_data,
        "zfs":         zfs_data,
        "smart":       smart_data,
        "docker":      dock_data,
        "system":      sys_data,
        "journal":     jrnl_data,
    }

    # ── Build report ───────────────────────────────────────────
    logger.info("Building report HTML and TXT...")
    html_body, txt_body = build_report(all_data, test_mode=test_mode)

    # ── Build subject ──────────────────────────────────────────
    period_str = f"{WEEK_START.strftime('%d %b')}–{NOW.strftime('%d %b %Y')}"
    prefix     = "[TEST] " if test_mode else ""
    subject    = f"{prefix}{HOMELAB_NAME} Weekly Report — {period_str}"

    # ── Handle modes ───────────────────────────────────────────
    if args.dry_run:
        save_dry_run_output(subject, html_body, txt_body)
        logger.info("Dry-run complete — no email sent")
        sys.exit(0)

    if test_mode:
        logger.info("Send-test mode — sending single test email")
        ok = send_report_email(subject, html_body, txt_body)
        sys.exit(0 if ok else 1)

    # ── Send real weekly report ────────────────────────────────
    logger.info(f"Sending weekly report to {EMAIL_TO}...")
    ok = send_report_email(subject, html_body, txt_body)
    if ok:
        logger.info("Weekly report sent successfully")
        sys.exit(0)
    else:
        logger.error("Weekly report send FAILED")
        sys.exit(1)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### reporting/.env.example

```bash
# =============================================================
# Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Report Environment
# Repo path: scripts/reporting/.env.example
# Live path: /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
#
# IMPORTANT:
#   Copy to .env and fill in real values.
#   NEVER commit .env to git.
#   chmod 600 .env && chown root:root .env
# =============================================================

# ── SMTP Configuration ─────────────────────────────────────────
# Gmail: use App Password (Google Account → Security → 2FA → App passwords)
SMTP_HOST=smtp.gmail.com
SMTP_PORT=587
SMTP_USERNAME=your-email@gmail.com
SMTP_PASSWORD=your-app-password-here
EMAIL_FROM=your-email@gmail.com
EMAIL_TO=your-email@gmail.com

# ── Homelab Identity ───────────────────────────────────────────
HOMELAB_NAME=Sovereign Homelab

# ── Proxmox API ────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Create a read-only API token in Proxmox:
# Datacenter → Permissions → API Tokens → Add
# Role: PVEAuditor (read-only)
# Format: USER@REALM!TOKENID
PROXMOX_HOST=proxmox.internal
PROXMOX_TOKEN_ID=root@pam!weekly-report
PROXMOX_TOKEN_SECRET=replace-with-your-proxmox-token-secret

# ── PBS API ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Create a read-only API token in PBS:
# Administration → API Tokens → Add
# Role: Audit
PBS_HOST=pbs.internal
PBS_TOKEN_ID=root@pam!weekly-report
PBS_TOKEN_SECRET=replace-with-your-pbs-token-secret

# ── Uptime Kuma SQLite path ────────────────────────────────────
# Default location inside Docker volume:
# KUMA_DB_PATH=/var/lib/docker/volumes/uptime-kuma_data/_data/kuma.db
# Or if mounted directly:
KUMA_DB_PATH=/opt/uptime-kuma/data/kuma.db
```

### reporting/systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.service

```ini
# =============================================================
# Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Report Systemd Service
# Repo path: scripts/reporting/systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.service
# Live path: /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-weekly-report.service
#
# Install:
#   cp sovereign-weekly-report.service /etc/systemd/system/
#   cp sovereign-weekly-report.timer   /etc/systemd/system/
#   systemctl daemon-reload
#   systemctl enable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer
#
# Manual run:
#   systemctl start sovereign-weekly-report
#
# Check:
#   systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer
#   journalctl -u sovereign-weekly-report -n 50
# =============================================================

[Unit]
Description=Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Status Report Generator & Sender
Documentation=https://github.com/Mohamed-DN/Sovereign-Homelab
After=network-online.target
Wants=network-online.target

[Service]
Type=oneshot
User=root
Group=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting
ExecStart=/usr/bin/python3 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py
StandardOutput=journal
StandardError=journal
SyslogIdentifier=sovereign-weekly-report

# Environment
EnvironmentFile=-/opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env

# Hardening
NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true
ProtectSystem=full
ProtectHome=true

# Allow write to state and log directories
# NOTE: if ProtectSystem=full causes issues reading /proc or running zpool,
#       change to ProtectSystem=strict and add ReadOnlyPaths as needed.
ReadWritePaths=/var/lib/sovereign-homelab /var/log/sovereign-homelab /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting

# Allow subprocess access to docker and system tools
# If docker fails inside service: add /var/run/docker.sock to ReadWritePaths
# ReadWritePaths=... /var/run/docker.sock

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
```

---

### reporting/systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.timer

```ini
# =============================================================
# Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Report Timer
# Repo path: scripts/reporting/systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.timer
# Live path: /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-weekly-report.timer
#
# Schedule: Every Monday at 09:00 Europe/Rome
#
# Install:
#   systemctl enable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer
#
# Verify:
#   systemctl list-timers | grep sovereign
#   systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer
#
# Force run now (testing):
#   systemctl start sovereign-weekly-report
# =============================================================

[Unit]
Description=Sovereign Homelab — Weekly Report Timer (Monday 09:00 Europe/Rome)
Documentation=https://github.com/Mohamed-DN/Sovereign-Homelab

[Timer]
# Every Monday at 09:00 local time (Europe/Rome)
OnCalendar=Mon *-*-* 09:00:00
# Timezone — adjust if your server is in UTC (common for Proxmox)
# If server is in UTC, use: OnCalendar=Mon *-*-* 08:00:00 (UTC+1 in winter)
# Or install systemd with timezone support and use:
# NOTE: systemd OnCalendar does NOT respect TZ natively in all versions.
# For reliable timezone: use a wrapper script or set the system timezone
# to Europe/Rome with: timedatectl set-timezone Europe/Rome
OnCalendar=Mon *-*-* 09:00:00

# Allow up to 15 minutes late start if system was off/busy
RandomizedDelaySec=300
AccuracySec=60

# Run immediately if the timer was missed (server was off on Monday morning)
Persistent=true

[Install]
WantedBy=timers.target
```

### Weekly report install commands

```bash
# ── 1. Create directories ──────────────────────────────────────
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/templates
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/systemd
mkdir -p /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output
mkdir -p /var/log/sovereign-homelab

# ── 2. Install Python dependencies ────────────────────────────
pip3 install requests python-dotenv

# ── 3. Copy script (paste content from above) ─────────────────
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py
chmod +x /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py

# ── 4. Copy template files ─────────────────────────────────────
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/templates/weekly_report.txt
# HTML template is embedded in the script as fallback.
# Optionally create external:
# nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/templates/weekly_report.html

# ── 5. Configure environment ───────────────────────────────────
cp /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env.example \
   /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
chmod 600 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
chown root:root /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env

# ── 6. Set server timezone (if not already set) ────────────────
timedatectl set-timezone Europe/Rome
timedatectl status

# ── 7. Test dry-run (no email) ─────────────────────────────────
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --dry-run
# Check output:
ls -la /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output/
# Open HTML in browser to verify:
# scp root@proxmox:/var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output/*.html ./

# ── 8. Test with real email ────────────────────────────────────
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --send-test
# Check inbox for subject: [TEST] Sovereign Homelab Weekly Report

# ── 9. Install systemd service and timer ──────────────────────
cp systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.service /etc/systemd/system/
cp systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.timer   /etc/systemd/system/
systemctl daemon-reload
systemctl enable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer

# ── 10. Verify timer is active ─────────────────────────────────
systemctl list-timers | grep sovereign
systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer

# ── 11. Force immediate run (manual test) ─────────────────────
systemctl start sovereign-weekly-report
journalctl -u sovereign-weekly-report -f

# ── 12. Rollback (if something breaks) ────────────────────────
systemctl disable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer
systemctl disable sovereign-weekly-report
rm /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-weekly-report.*
systemctl daemon-reload
```

## 15. install/INSTALL_DASHBOARD.md

```markdown
# Install: Homepage Dashboard

## Prerequisites

- Homepage running in Docker Compose
- SSH access to LXC 101 (platform-services)
- Docker Compose path: /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/

## Step 1 — Backup current files

```bash
BACKUP_TS=$(date +%F-%H%M)
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage

cp services.yaml  services.yaml.bak-$BACKUP_TS
cp settings.yaml  settings.yaml.bak-$BACKUP_TS
cp bookmarks.yaml bookmarks.yaml.bak-$BACKUP_TS

# CSS may not exist yet
[ -f custom.css ] && cp custom.css custom.css.bak-$BACKUP_TS || echo "custom.css not found — will be created"
```

## Step 2 — Edit each file

```bash
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/services.yaml
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/settings.yaml
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/bookmarks.yaml
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/custom.css
```

Paste each file content from this output package.

## Step 3 — Reload Homepage

```bash
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability
docker compose restart homepage
```

## Step 4 — Validate

```bash
# Wait 5 seconds for restart
sleep 5

# Check HTTP response
curl -sI http://dash.internal | head -5

# Check logs
docker compose logs homepage --tail=30

# Check container status
docker compose ps homepage
```

Expected output:
```
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
```

## Step 5 — Rollback if broken

```bash
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage
cp services.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM  services.yaml
cp settings.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM  settings.yaml
cp bookmarks.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM bookmarks.yaml
cd ..
docker compose restart homepage
```

## Notes on siteMonitor

Services with `ping:` instead of `siteMonitor:` use ICMP ping — more reliable for
services behind auth walls. Services with `siteMonitor:` must return HTTP 200 without
redirect to show green. If a service shows red when you know it is working, remove
its `siteMonitor:` line and add `ping:` instead.
```

# Install: Alert Relay

## Architecture

```
Uptime Kuma → POST /webhook → alert_relay.py:5001 → wait 60s → HTML email

## Step 4 — Configure environment

   /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env

nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
# Fill in: SMTP_HOST, SMTP_PORT, SMTP_USERNAME, SMTP_PASSWORD, EMAIL_FROM, EMAIL_TO

chmod 600 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
chown root:root /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env
```

## Step 5 — Test dry-run

```bash
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting
python3 send_test_alert.py --type down --service Immich --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type resolved --service Immich --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type test --dry-run

# Check output files were created:
ls -la /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/alerting/dry_run_output/
```

## Step 6 — Send real test email

```bash
python3 send_test_alert.py --type test
# Check Gmail inbox for subject: [TEST] 🔔 Alert Relay Test
```

## Step 7 — Install systemd service

```bash
cp /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/systemd/sovereign-alert-relay.service \
   /etc/systemd/system/
systemctl daemon-reload
systemctl enable --now sovereign-alert-relay
systemctl status sovereign-alert-relay
```

## Step 8 — Configure Uptime Kuma webhook

1. Open Uptime Kuma: http://status.internal
2. Settings → Notifications → Add Notification
3. Type: **Webhook**
4. Friendly Name: `Alert Relay`
5. URL: `http://127.0.0.1:5001/webhook`
   - Use 127.0.0.1 if Kuma and relay are on the same LXC
   - Use LXC 101 IP if they are on different containers
6. Request body: `JSON` (default)
7. Test the notification from Kuma

## Step 9 — Verify end-to-end

```bash
# Check relay health
curl http://127.0.0.1:5001/health

# Check active incidents
curl http://127.0.0.1:5001/incidents

# Watch logs
journalctl -u sovereign-alert-relay -f

# Simulate a webhook (manual test):
curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:5001/webhook \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"heartbeat":{"status":0,"time":"2025-06-01T10:00:00Z","msg":"timeout"},"monitor":{"id":1,"name":"TestService"}}'
# Wait 60s — check if email arrives
```

## Rollback

```bash
systemctl disable --now sovereign-alert-relay
rm /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-alert-relay.service
systemctl daemon-reload
# Remove Kuma notification in Uptime Kuma UI
```
```

## 15c. install/INSTALL_WEEKLY_REPORT.md

```markdown
# Install: Weekly Report

## Step 1 — Install dependencies

```bash
pip3 install requests python-dotenv
```

## Step 2 — Create directories

```bash
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/templates
mkdir -p /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/systemd
mkdir -p /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output
mkdir -p /var/log/sovereign-homelab
```

## Step 3 — Copy files

```bash
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/templates/weekly_report.txt
chmod +x /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/weekly_homelab_report.py
```

## Step 4 — Configure environment

```bash
cp /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env.example \
   /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
nano /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
chmod 600 /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
chown root:root /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env
```

## Step 5 — Proxmox & PBS API tokens (optional but recommended)

### Proxmox read-only token:
1. Proxmox UI → Datacenter → Permissions → API Tokens → Add
2. User: root@pam (or a dedicated user)
3. Token ID: weekly-report
4. Privilege Separation: YES (important)
5. Assign role PVEAuditor to token at / path

### PBS read-only token:
1. PBS UI → Administration → API Tokens → Add
2. Token ID: weekly-report
3. Assign role Audit

Copy token secrets into `.env`.

## Step 6 — Uptime Kuma DB path

Find the correct path:
```bash
# If using Docker volume:
docker volume inspect uptime-kuma_data
# Look for Mountpoint, then add /kuma.db

# Common paths:
ls /var/lib/docker/volumes/uptime-kuma_data/_data/kuma.db
ls /opt/uptime-kuma/data/kuma.db
```
Set `KUMA_DB_PATH` in `.env`.

## Step 7 — Set timezone

```bash
timedatectl set-timezone Europe/Rome
timedatectl status
```

## Step 8 — Dry-run test

```bash
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --dry-run

# View HTML output
ls /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output/
# Copy HTML to local machine for visual inspection
```

## Step 9 — Send test email

```bash
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --send-test
# Check inbox for: [TEST] Sovereign Homelab Weekly Report
```

## Step 10 — Install systemd timer

```bash
cp systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.service /etc/systemd/system/
cp systemd/sovereign-weekly-report.timer   /etc/systemd/system/
systemctl daemon-reload
systemctl enable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer

# Verify
systemctl list-timers | grep sovereign
systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer
```

## Step 11 — Force immediate run

```bash
systemctl start sovereign-weekly-report
journalctl -u sovereign-weekly-report -n 100
```

## Rollback

```bash
systemctl disable --now sovereign-weekly-report.timer
systemctl disable sovereign-weekly-report
rm /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-weekly-report.*
systemctl daemon-reload
```

# Rollback Procedures

## Dashboard Rollback

```bash
# Find backup files:
ls /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/*.bak-*

# Restore (replace YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM with actual timestamp):
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage
cp services.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM  services.yaml
cp settings.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM  settings.yaml
cp bookmarks.yaml.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM bookmarks.yaml
cp custom.css.bak-YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM     custom.css

# Reload:
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability
docker compose restart homepage

# Verify:
curl -sI http://dash.internal | head -3
```

```bash
# Stop and disable service:
systemctl disable --now sovereign-alert-relay

# Remove service file:
rm /etc/systemd/system/sovereign-alert-relay.service

# Remove webhook in Uptime Kuma:
# Uptime Kuma UI → Settings → Notifications → delete "Alert Relay"

# Optionally remove scripts:

```

# Stop timer:

# Optionally remove scripts:

```

# Dry-run outputs:

## 16. Validation Commands (complete)

```bash
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════
# DASHBOARD VALIDATION
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 1. Check HTTP response
curl -sI http://dash.internal | head -5

# 2. Check Docker container is running
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability
docker compose ps homepage

# 3. Check logs for YAML parse errors
docker compose logs homepage --tail=50 | grep -iE "error|warn|yaml|config"

# 4. Check config files syntax (optional: install yamllint)
yamllint /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/services.yaml
yamllint /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/settings.yaml
yamllint /opt/sovereign-homelab/stacks/observability/homepage/bookmarks.yaml

# 5. Verify custom.css is served
curl -sI http://dash.internal/custom.css


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════
# ALERTING VALIDATION
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 1. Check relay is listening
curl -s http://127.0.0.1:5001/health | python3 -m json.tool

# 2. Check active incidents
curl -s http://127.0.0.1:5001/incidents | python3 -m json.tool

# 3. Dry-run test alert
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting
python3 send_test_alert.py --type down      --service Immich    --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type reminder  --service Nextcloud --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type resolved  --service Immich    --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type warning   --service Forgejo   --dry-run
python3 send_test_alert.py --type test                          --dry-run

# 4. Check dry-run outputs were created
ls -la /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/alerting/dry_run_output/

# 5. Send real test email
python3 send_test_alert.py --type test
# → Check Gmail inbox

# 6. Simulate webhook manually
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:5001/webhook \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "heartbeat": {"status": 0, "time": "2025-01-01T10:00:00Z", "msg": "timeout"},
    "monitor":   {"id": 99, "name": "Immich"}
  }'

# 7. Check systemd service status
systemctl status sovereign-alert-relay
journalctl -u sovereign-alert-relay -n 100 --no-pager

# 8. Check relay is not exposed externally
# This should FAIL (connection refused) — relay is localhost only
curl -m 3 http://YOUR_SERVER_IP:5001/health && echo "WARNING: relay is public!" || echo "OK: relay is localhost only"


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════
# WEEKLY REPORT VALIDATION
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 1. Dry-run (no email)
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --dry-run

# 2. Check output files
ls -la /var/lib/sovereign-homelab/reporting/dry_run_output/

# 3. Send test email
python3 weekly_homelab_report.py --send-test
# → Check inbox for [TEST] prefix

# 4. Check timer is active
systemctl list-timers | grep sovereign
systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer

# 5. Check when next run is scheduled
systemctl status sovereign-weekly-report.timer | grep "Next elapse"

# 6. Force immediate run (manual)
systemctl start sovereign-weekly-report
journalctl -u sovereign-weekly-report -n 100 --no-pager

# 7. Check log file
tail -50 /var/log/sovereign-homelab/weekly_report.log


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════
# SECRETS SAFETY CHECK
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 1. Check no secrets in git-tracked files
cd /opt/sovereign-homelab
git status --short
git diff --check

# 2. Check no passwords in scripts (should find only PLACEHOLDER text)
grep -rn "SMTP_PASSWORD\|TOKEN_SECRET\|API_KEY" scripts/ \
  --include="*.py" --include="*.sh" --include="*.yaml" \
  | grep -v "\.env\|example\|placeholder\|your-"

# 3. Verify .env files have correct permissions
stat /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/alerting/.env  | grep "Access:"
stat /opt/sovereign-homelab/scripts/reporting/.env | grep "Access:"
# Expected: Access: (0600/-rw-------)

# 4. Confirm .env is in .gitignore
grep "\.env" /opt/sovereign-homelab/.gitignore

# 5. Check no .env committed accidentally
git ls-files | grep "\.env$"
# Should return nothing


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════
# SYSTEM HEALTH CHECK (run on Proxmox host)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════

# ZFS
zpool status -v
zfs list

# SMART
smartctl -a /dev/sda | grep -E "SMART overall|Reallocated|Pending|Uncorrectable"
# Or use Scrutiny: http://disks.internal

# Failed systemd units
systemctl --failed

# Proxmox tasks
pvesh get /nodes/pve/tasks --limit 20

# PBS storage
pvesm status
# Or from PBS: https://pbs.internal:8007

# Docker containers
docker ps -a --format "table {{.Names}}\t{{.Status}}\t{{.RunningFor}}"

# Network connectivity
curl -sI http://status.internal  | head -3   # Uptime Kuma
curl -sI http://adguard.internal | head -3   # AdGuard
curl -sI http://npm.internal     | head -3   # NPM
curl -s  https://vpn.casca-certosa.duckdns.org/health  # Headscale public
```
